hṛtpadme saṃsthitā nityam 
hṛtpadme suranāyike 
hṛdayaṃ ca daśākṣaram 
hṛdayaṃ tu saraḥ proktaṃ 
hṛdayaṃ śuṣyate yasya 
hṛdayaṃ sarvamantrāṇāṃ 
hṛdayādiprabhedena 
hṛdayādyastraparyantam 
hṛdaye tu mahākālam 
hṛdayena tu devyāyāḥ 
hṛdaye mṛtyubhāg bhavet 
hṛdaye yasya santāpaṃ 
hṛdaye yaḥ sthito granthis 
hṛdaye sarvajantuṣu 
hṛdādau kramaśo vṛddhyā 
hṛdi kṛtvā kujeśvaram 
hṛdi gūḍhaṃ parāparam 
hṛdi pādau ca śuṣyati 
hṛdisthaṃ ca anāhatam 
hṛdisthaḥ parameśvaraḥ 
hṛdisthā sampravartate 
hṛdyordhvaghaṭa-m-antare 
hṛnnādaṃ manasotthāpya 
hṛnnābhau liṅgamadhyagam 
hṛnmadhye cintayec cakraṃ 
hṛllekhe paramānande 
hetutarkavivarjitam 
hemaprākāramaṇḍitam 
heyopāyavinirmuktaṃ 
herambo dhūlisaṃjñas tu 
heriyugmaṃ smṛtaṃ bhadre 
helayā cāṇimāṣṭakam 
helayā maṇḍalaṃ tu tam 
helāgamanamārgeṇa 
helādolaikatatparaḥ 
helādolair vyavasthitam 
helā nāmeti cocyate 
helā lolā tathā līlā 
homamaṇḍalakaṃ yac ca 
hrasvā tyājyā prayatnena 
hrasve nīle bhayaṃ vindyād 
hrāsyamānā pade pade 
hrīṃ hūṃ svleṃ svāhāpataye
